First time at this Vital location was this past Sunday and my husband and I enjoyed this gym -- the routes were fun and offered challenges. We recently joined in on my brother-in-law's family plan and got our annual membership on Black Friday to the Vital gyms (great deal and very excited about our new memberships!). <Response>None</Response>< review>
I'm a member, I go climbing 3 times a week. This is one of their smaller locations -they recently opened a new spot in Oceanside with a LOT of space. But I've made my little community here. Climbers and staff alike are super friendly, if you ask for help they'll help you out. The staff here are knowledgeable about climbing and everyone just wants to have a good time.
Parking can be difficult sometimes, thee are dance studios next door and a LOT of parents waiting and blocking space when dance class is ending, but if you have to walk a bit farther it's still not too far. But the flip side is sometimes you show up and it's empty.
Open hours are 11 AM to 9 PM, then as a member you get 24 hour access. Which is another huge perk. I love the opportunity to climb early in the morning or late at night depending on my schedule.</review>

<user>108960625154492973625< /user><Name>Kenny Hansell</Name><date>1557602810771</date>< rate>
5</rate>
<Text>I just completed the 6 week challenge with DC fitness. It was a total success - so I wanted to share my story to not only show appreciation for the program, but to also advise others others look to achieve their fitness goals.

Moving to LA a year and a half ago was difficult. It was a move I had to make, but the challenges that come with a cross country move took a toll on my mind and body.

2 months ago, I came across one of those Instagram ads about getting fit in 6 weeks. I was skeptical, but I needed to get fit. As a constant athlete growing up, I was not happy with where my body was at and needed a change. So I put the money down and was all in.

The program offers 3 main facets: Fitness, Nutrition, and Accountability.  Working out 3 times a week with the DC team ended up becoming some I looked forward to, rather that something I dreaded. This was because It was only a 45 minute-1 hour work out where I knew I would maximize my time. I was able to build great relationships with each trainer, who truly cared able my progress and success. I was surprised by how supportive all the other gym members were as well - but I guess that what happens when there is a mutual goal.

Stay true to the regiment this program lays out for you, and you will see results in 6 weeks. I recommend the challenge to anybody looking to improve their physical and mental health, through a challenge that provides all the necessary tools to succeed.
